### <a id="inductive-types-h-s-p-and-v">Inductive Types H, S, P, and V</a>

This section presents the [UALib.Varieties.Varieties][] module of the [Agda Universal Algebra Library][].

Fix a signature 𝑆, let 𝒦 be a class of 𝑆-algebras, and define

* H 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a homomorphic image of a members of 𝒦;
* S 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a subalgebra of a member of 𝒦;
* P 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a product of members of 𝒦.

A straight-forward verification confirms that H, S, and P are **closure operators** (expansive, monotone, and idempotent).  A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is said to be *closed under the taking of homomorphic images* provided `H 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. Similarly, 𝒦 is *closed under the taking of subalgebras* (resp., *arbitrary products*) provided `S 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦` (resp., `P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`). The operators H, S, and P can be composed with one another repeatedly, forming yet more closure operators.

An algebra is a homomorphic image (resp., subalgebra; resp., product) of every algebra to which it is isomorphic. Thus, the class `H 𝒦` (resp., `S 𝒦`; resp., `P 𝒦`) is closed under isomorphism.

A **variety** is a class of algebras, in the same signature, that is closed under the taking of homomorphic images, subalgebras, and arbitrary products.  To represent varieties we define inductive types for the closure operators `H`, `S`, and `P` that are composable.  Separately, we define an inductive type `V` which simultaneously represents closure under all three operators, `H`, `S`, and `P`.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="1654" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="1658" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="1666" class="Pragma">--without-K</a> <a id="1678" class="Pragma">--exact-split</a> <a id="1692" class="Pragma">--safe</a> <a id="1699" class="Symbol">#-}</a>

#### <a id="homomorphic-closure">Homomorphic closure</a>

We define the inductive type `H` to represent classes of algebras that include all homomorphic images of algebras in the class; i.e., classes that are closed under the taking of homomorphic images.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="2377" class="Comment">--Closure wrt H</a>
<a id="2393" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="H"></a><a id="2398" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2398" class="Datatype">H</a> <a id="2400" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2401" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2401" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="2403" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2403" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="2405" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2407" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="2415" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="2417" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2417" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="2419" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2421" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1088" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="2426" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2427" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#781" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="2435" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2401" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="2437" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="2438" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="2440" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2005" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="2443" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2401" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="2444" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="2447" class="Symbol">:</a>

  <a id="H.hiso"></a><a id="2694" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">hiso</a>  <a id="2700" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2702" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2703" #### <a id="subalgebraic-closure">Subalgebraic closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing the semantic notion of a class of algebras that is closed under the taking of subalgebras is the following.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="3068" class="Comment">--Closure wrt S</a>
<a id="3084" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="S"></a><a id="3089" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3089" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="3091" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3092" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3092" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3094" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3094" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="3096" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3098" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="3106" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="3108" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3108" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="3110" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3112" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1088" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="3117" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3118" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#781" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3126" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3092" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3128" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3129" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3131" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3132" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2005" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="3135" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3092" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="3136" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="3139" class="Symbol">:</a>
 <a id="3142" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1088" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="3147" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3148" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#781" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3156" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3157" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3092" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3159" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="3161" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3094" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3162" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3164" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3165" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3167" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3168" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2005" class="Function">ov</a><a id="3170" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3171" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3092" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3173" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="3175" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3094" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3176" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="3179" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="S.sbase"></a><a id="3187" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3187" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="3193" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3195" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3196" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3196" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3198" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3200" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#781" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3208" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3092" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3210" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3211" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3213" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3215" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3196" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3217" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2725" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="3219" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3108" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="3221" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3223" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#4626" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="3232" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3196" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3234" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3094" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="3236" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2725" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="3238" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3089" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="3240" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3108" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3108" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

-----------------------------------------

#### <a id="product-closure">Product closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing the semantic notion of an class of algebras closed under the taking of arbitrary products is the following.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="3825" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="P"></a><a id="3830" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3830" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="3832" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3833" <a id="3853" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1088" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="3858" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3859" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#781" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3867" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3833" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3869" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3870" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="3872" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3881" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1088" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="3886" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3887" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#781" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3895" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3896" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3833" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3898" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="3900" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3835" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3901" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3903" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4191" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4193" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3849" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="4194" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4196" class="Symbol">→</a> <a href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3849" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="P.prodw"></a><a id="4210" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4210" class="InductiveConstructor">prodw</a>  <a id="4217" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4219" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4220" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4246" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="4248" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4249" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4251" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4253" class="Symbol">(∀</a> <a id="4256" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4256" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="4258" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4260" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4266" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2725" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4268" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3830" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="4269" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4274" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4276" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3849" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="4277" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4279" class="Symbol">→</a> <a   <a id="P.pisou"></a><a id="4293" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4293" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a>  <a id="4300" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4302" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4303" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4365" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2725" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4367" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3830" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4369"   <a id="P.pisow"></a><a id="4373" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4373" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a>  <a id="4380" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4382" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4383" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4383" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4385" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4385" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4387" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4389" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#781" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4397" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="4399" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4400" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4402" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4404" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4383" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4406" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2725" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4408" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3830" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="4409" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4410" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3833" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4411" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4413" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3835" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4414" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4416" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3849" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4418" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4420" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4383" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4422" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4424" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4385" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4426" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4428" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4385" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4430" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2725" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4432" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3830" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4434" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3849" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

<!-- A class 𝒦 is **closed under** `P` (or `P`-**closed**) provided `P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. -->

-----------------------------------------------

#### <a id="varietal-closure">Varietal closure</a>

A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is called a **variety** if it is closed under each of the closure operators H, S, and P introduced above; the corresponding closure operator is often denoted 𝕍, but we will denote it by `V`.

We now define `V` as an inductive type.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="4905" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="V"></a><a id="4910" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4910" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="4912" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4913" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4913" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4915" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4915" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="4917" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4919" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="4927" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="4929" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4929" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4931" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4933" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1088" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="4938" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4939" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#781" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4947" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4913" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4949" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4950" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="4952" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2005" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="4955" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4913" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4956" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="4959" class="Symbol">:</a>
 <a id="4962" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1088" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="4967" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4968" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#781" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4976" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4977" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4913" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4979" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4981" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4915" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4982" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4984" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4985" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="4987" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2005" class="Function">ov</a><a id="4989" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4990" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4913" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4992" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4994" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4915" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4995" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="4998" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="V.vbase"></a><a id="5006" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5006" class="InductiveConstructor">vbase</a>  <a id="5013" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5015" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5016" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5016" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5018" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5020" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#781" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5028" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4913" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5030" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5031" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5033" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5035" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5016" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5037" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2725" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5039" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4929" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5041" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5043" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#4626" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="5052" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5016" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5054" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4915" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="5056" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2725" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5058" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4910" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5060" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4929" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

  <a id="V.vssubw"></a><a id="5361" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5361" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="5368" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5370" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5371" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5371" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5373" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5373" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5375" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5377" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#781" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5385" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="5387" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5388" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5390" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5392" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5371" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5394" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2725" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5396" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4910" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5397" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5398" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4913" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5399" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5401" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4915" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5402" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5404" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4929" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5406" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5408" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5373" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5410" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#3606" class="Function Operator">≤</a> <a id="5412" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5371" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5414" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5416" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5373" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5418" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2725" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5420" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4910" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5422" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4929" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5600" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5638" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2725" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5640" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5650" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5652" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5600" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5654" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="5656" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5617" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5658" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5660" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5617" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5662" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2725" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5664" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4910" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5666" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4929" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="V.visow"></a><a id="5670" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5670" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a>  <a id="5677" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5679" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5680" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5680" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5682" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5682" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5684" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5686" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#781" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5694" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="5696" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5697" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5699" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5701" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5680" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5703" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2725" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5705" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4910" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5706" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5707" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4913" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5708" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5710" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4915" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5711" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5713" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4929" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5715" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5717" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5680" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5719" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="5721" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5682" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5723" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5725" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5682" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5727" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2725" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5729" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4910" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5731" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4929" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

Thus, if 𝒦 is a class of 𝑆-algebras, then the **variety generated by** 𝒦 is denoted by `V 𝒦` and defined to be the smallest class that contains 𝒦 and is closed under `H`, `S`, and `P`.

With the closure operator V representing closure under HSP, we represent formally what it means to be a variety of algebras as follows.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="is-variety"></a><a id="6083" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6083" class="Function">is-variety</a> <a id="6094" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6096" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6097" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6097" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6099" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6101" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="6109" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="6111" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6111" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="6113" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6115" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1088" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="6120" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6121" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#781" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="6129" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6097" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6131" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="6132" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="6134" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2005" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6137" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6097" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6138" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="6141" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6143" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2005" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6146" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6097" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6148" href="universes.html#758" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="6150" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6083" class="Function">is-variety</a><a id="6160" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6161" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6161" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6162" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6164" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6164" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="6166" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6168" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4910" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="6169" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6170" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6161" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6171" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6173" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6161" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6174" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6176" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6164" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="6178" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#3007" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="6180" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6164" class="Bound">𝒱</a>

<a id="variety"></a><a id="6183" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6183" class="Function">variety</a> <a id="6191" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6193" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6194" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6194" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6196" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6198" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="6206" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6208" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6210" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6211" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2005" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6214" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6194" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6215" class="Symbol">)</a><a id="6216" href="universes.html#527" class="Function Operator">⁺</a> <a id="6218" href="universes.html#758" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="6220" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6183" class="Function">variety</a> <a id="6228" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6228" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6230" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6232" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="6234" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6234" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="6236" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="6238" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6239" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1088" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="6244" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6245" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#781" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="6253" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6228" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6255" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="6256" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="6258" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2005" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6261" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6228" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6262" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="6265" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="6267" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6083" class="Function">is-variety</a> <a id="6278" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6234" class="Bound">𝒱</a>

</pre>



-------------------------------

#### <a id="closure-properties">Closure properties</a>

The types defined above represent operators with useful closure properties. We now prove a handful of such properties that we need later.

First, `P` is a closure operator.  This is proved by checking that `P` is *monotone*, *expansive*, and *idempotent*. The meaning of these terms will be clear from the definitions of the types that follow.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="P-mono"></a><a id="6743" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6743" class="Function">P-mono</a> <a id="6750" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6752" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6753" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6753" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6755" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6755" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="6757" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6759" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="6767" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6769" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6769" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="6771" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6771" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a> <a id="6774" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6776" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1088" class="Function">Pred</a><a id="6780" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6781" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#781" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="6789" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6753" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6791" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="6792" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="6794" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2005" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6797" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6753" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6798" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="6801" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6803" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6769" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="6805" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#3007" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="6807" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6771" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a> <a id="6810" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6812" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3830" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="6813" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6814" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6753" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6815" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6817" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6755" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="6818" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6820" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6829" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6755" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="6830" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6832" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6771" <a id="7753" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7346" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="7761" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7762" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7762" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="7763" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7765" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7765" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="7766" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7768" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7769" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4293" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a> <a id="7775" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7775" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7777" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7777" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="7779" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7781" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7783" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4373" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="7789" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7790" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7346" class="Function">P-idemp</a><a id="7797" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7798" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7762" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="7799" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7801" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7765" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="7802" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7804" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7775" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7805" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7807" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7777" class="Bound">x₁</a>
<a id="7810" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7346" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="7818" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7819" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7819" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="7820" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7822" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7822" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="7823" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7825" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7826" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4373" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="7832" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7832" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7834" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7834" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="7836" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7838" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7840" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4373" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="7846" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7847" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7346" class="Function">P-idemp</a><a id="7854" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7855" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7819" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="7856" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7858" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7822" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="7859" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7861" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7832" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7862" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7864" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7834" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>

Similarly, S is a closure operator.  The facts that S is idempotent and expansive won't be needed below, so we omit these, but we will make use of monotonicity of S.  Here is the proof of the latter.

<pre class="Agda">

We sometimes want to go back and forth between our two representations of subalgebras of algebras in a class. The tools `subalgebra→S` and `S→subalgebra` are made for that purpose.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="subalgebra→S"></a><a id="8677" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8677" class="Function">subalgebra→S</a> <a id="8690" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8692" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8693" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8693" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8695" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8695" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="8697" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8699" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="8707" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8709" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8709" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="8711" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8713" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1088" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="8718" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8719" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#781" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="8727" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8693" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8729" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="8730" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="8732" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2005" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="8735" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8693" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="8736" class="Symbol">)}{</a><a id="8739" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8739" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="8741" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8743" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#781" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="8751" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8752" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8693" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8754" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="8756" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8695" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="8757" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8759" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="8760" class="Symbol">}</a>
 <a id="8763" class="Symbol">→</a>             <a id="8777" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8739" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="8779" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#3799" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="8799" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8709" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
               <a id="8816" class="Comment">------------------------</a>
 <a id="8842" class="Symbol">→</a>             <a id="8856" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8739" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="8858" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2725" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="8860" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3089" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="8861" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8862" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8693" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="8863" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8865" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8695" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="8866" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8868" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8709" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

<a id="8871" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8677" class="Function">subalgebra→S</a> <a id="8884" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8885" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8885" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="8886" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8888" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8888" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="8889" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8891" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8891" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="8892" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8894" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8894" class="Bound">𝑪</a><a id="8895" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8897" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8898" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8898" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="8900" href="MGS-MLTT.html#2929" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8902" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="8904" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8904" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="8906" href="MGS-MLTT.html#2929" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8908" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8908" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="8911" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8913" href="MGS-MLTT.html#2929" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8915" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8915" class="Bound">KA</a> <a id="8918" href="MGS-MLTT.html#2929" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8920" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8920" class="Bound">C≅B</a><a id="8923" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="8926" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8928" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3309" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a> <a id="8933" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9043" class="Function">sA</a> <a id="8936" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8949" class="Function">C≤A</a>

  <a id="8949" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8949" class="Function">C≤A</a> <a id="8953" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8955" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8894" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="8957" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#3606" class="Function Operator">≤</a> <a id="8959" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8898" class="Bound">𝑨</a>

</pre>

Next we observe that lifting to a higher universe does not break the property of being a subalgebra of an algebra of a class.  In other words, if we lift a subalgebra of an algebra in a class, the result is still a subalgebra of an algebra in the class.

<pre class="Agda">

  <a id="11198" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11153" class="Function">lC</a> <a id="11201" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11203" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#4626" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="11212" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11064" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="11214" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11050" class="Bound">𝓦</a>

  <a id="11219" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11219" class="Function">lC≤lA</a> <a id="11225" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11227" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11153" class="Function">lC</a> <a id="11230" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#3606" class="Function Operator">≤</a> <a id="11232" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11150" class="Function">lA</a>
  <a id="11237" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11219" class="Function">lC≤lA</a> <a id="11243" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11245" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#8771" class="Function">lift-alg-≤</a> <a id="11256" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11064" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="11258" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11259" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11059" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="11260" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11262" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11068" class="Bound">C≤A</a>
  <a id="11268" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11268" class="Function">plA</a> <a id="11272" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11274" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11150" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="11277" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2725" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="11279" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3830" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="11280" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11281" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11047" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="11282" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="11284" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11050" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="11285" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11287" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11053" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="11291" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11268" class="Function">plA</a> <a id="11295" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11297" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3983" class="InductiveConstructor">pliftu</a> <a id="11304" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11075" class="Bound">pA</a>

</pre>

The next lemma would be too obvoius to care about were it not for the fact that we'll need it later, so it too must be formalized.

We need to formalize one more lemma before arriving the main objective of this section, which is the proof of the inclusion PS⊆SP.

<pre class="Agda">

  <a id="13876" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13854" class="Function">⨅SA≤⨅𝒜</a> <a id="13883" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13885" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13886" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13628" class="Function">α</a> <a id="13888" href="MGS-MLTT.html#2929" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13890" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13679" class="Function">β</a><a id="13891" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13893" href="MGS-MLTT.html#2929" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13895" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13773" class="Function">γ</a>

</pre>

#### <a id="PS-in-SP">PS(𝒦) ⊆ SP(𝒦)</a>

Finally, we are in a position to prove that a product of subalgebras of algebras in a class 𝒦 is a subalgebra of a product of algebras in 𝒦.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="14172" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="14179" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14179" class="Module">_</a> <a id="14181" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14182" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14182" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="14184" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14186" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="14194" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14196" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14196" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="14198" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14200" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1088" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="14205" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14206" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#781" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="14214" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14182" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="14216" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="14217" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="14219" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2005" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="14222" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14182" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14223" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="14226" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14227" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14227" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="14231" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14233" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a> <a id="14241" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14242" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2005" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="14245" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14182" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14246" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="14248" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2005" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="14251" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14182" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14252" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="14255" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="14263" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14263" class="Function">ov𝓾</a> <a id="14267" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14269" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a>
 <a id="14279" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14263" class="Function">ov𝓾</a> <a id="14283" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14285" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2005" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="14288" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14182" class="Bound">𝓤</a>

   <a id="15252" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15252" class="Function">η</a> <a id="15254" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15256" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#1031" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="15258" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15103" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="15260" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#3799" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="15280" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15281" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3830" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="15282" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15283" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14263" class="Function">ov𝓾</a><a id="15286" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="15288" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14263" class="Function">ov𝓾</a><a id="15291" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15293" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15294" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3830" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="15295" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15296" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14182" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="15297" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="15299" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14263" class="Function">ov𝓾</a><a id="15302" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15304" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14196" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="15305" class="Symbol">))</a>
   <a id="15311" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15252" class="Function">η</a> <a id="15313" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15315" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12981" class="Function">lemPS⊆SP</a><a id="15323" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15324" class="Argument">𝓤</a> <a id="15326" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15328" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14263" class="Function">ov𝓾</a><a id="15331" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="15333" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14263" class="Function">ov𝓾</a><a id="15336" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="15338" class="Argument">𝒦</a> <a id="15340" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15342" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15343" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3830" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="15345" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14196" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="15346" class="Symbol">)}{</a><a id="15349" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14227" class="Bound">hfe</a><a id="15352" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="15354" class="Argument">I</a> <a id="15356" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15358" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15100" class="Bound">I</a><a id="15359" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="15361" class="Argument">ℬ</a> <a id="15363" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15365" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15103" class="Bound">𝒜</a><a id="15366" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15368" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15158" class="Function">ξ</a>

</pre>

#### <a id="more-class-inclusions">More class inclusions</a>

We conclude this module with three more inclusion relations that will have bit parts to play later (e.g., in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem).

<a id="16244" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16053" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="16249" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16250" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3309" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a><a id="16254" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16255" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16255" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="16256" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16258" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16258" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="16259" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16261" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16261" class="Bound">spA</a> <a id="16265" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16265" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="16268" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16270" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16272" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5361" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="16279" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16280" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16053" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="16285" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16261" class="Bound">spA</a><a id="16288" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16290" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16265" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="16294" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16053" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="16299" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16300" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3388" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a><a id="16305" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16306" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16306" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="16307" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16309" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16309" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="16310" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16312" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16312" class="Bound">spA</a> <a id="16316" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16316" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="16319" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16321" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16323" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5361" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="16330" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16331" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16053" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="16336" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16312" class="Bound">spA</a><a id="16339" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16341" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16316" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="16345" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16053" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="16350" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16351" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3452" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="16356" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16356" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16358" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16358" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="16360" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16362" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16364" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5670" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="16370" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16371" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16053" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="16376" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16356" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16377" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16379" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16358" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>


#### <a id="S-in-SP">⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦)</a>

Finally, we prove the result that plays an important role, e.g., in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem. As we saw in [Algebras.Products][], the (informal) product `⨅ S(𝒦)` of all subalgebras of algebras in 𝒦 is implemented (formally) in the [UALib][] as `⨅ 𝔄 S(𝒦)`. Our goal is to prove that this product belongs to `SP(𝒦)`. We do so by first proving that the product belongs to `PS(𝒦)` and then applying the `PS⊆SP` lemma.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="class-prod-s-∈-ps"></a><a id="16880" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16880" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="16898" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16900" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16901" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16901" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="16903" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16905" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="16913" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16915" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16915" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="16917" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16919" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16901" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="16921" href="universes.html#758" class="Function Operator">̇</a><a id="16922" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16924" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16924" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="16926" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16928" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1088" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="16933" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16934" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#781" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="16942" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16901" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="16944" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="16945" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="16947" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2005" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="16950" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16901" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16951" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="16955" class="Symbol">→</a>                  <a id="16974" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#3890" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="16988" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16989" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16901" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16990" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16992" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16901" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16993" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16995" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16915" class="Bound">X</a><a id="16996" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16998" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16999" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3089" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="17001" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16924" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="17002" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17004" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2725" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="17006" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17007" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3830" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="17008" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17009" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2005" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="17012" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16901" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17013" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17015" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2005" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="17018" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16901" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17019" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17021" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17022" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3089" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="17024" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16924" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="17025" class="Symbol">))</a>

<a id="17029" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16880" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="17047" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17048" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17048" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17049" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17051" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17051" class="Bound">X</a><a id="17052" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17054" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17054" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="17055" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="17058" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17060" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4293" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a> <a id="17066" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17334" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="17073" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17074" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6367" class="Function">⨅≅</a> <a id="17077" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1901" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="17081" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17385" class="Function">llA≅A</a><a id="17086" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="17385" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17385" class="Function">llA≅A</a> <a id="17391" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17393" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="17395" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17395" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="17397" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17399" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17400" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17100" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="17404" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17395" class="Bound">i</a><a id="17405" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17407" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="17409" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17410" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#3667" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="17412" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17413" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3089" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="17415" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17054" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="17416" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17418" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17395" class="Bound">i</a><a id="17419" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="17423" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17385" class="Function">llA≅A</a> <a id="17429" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17429" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="17431" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17433" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3896" class="Function">Trans-≅</a> <a id="17441" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17442" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17100" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="17446" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17429" class="Bound">i</a><a id="17447" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17449" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17450" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#3667" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="17452" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17453" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3089" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="17455" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17054" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="17456" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17458" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17429" class="Bound">i</a><a id="17459" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17461" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17462" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2465" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="17468" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4457" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="17478" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17480" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17481" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2465" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="17487" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4457" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="17497" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="17500" class="Comment">-- So, since PS⊆SP, we see that that the product of all subalgebras of a class 𝒦 belongs to SP(𝒦).</a>
<a id="class-prod-s-∈-sp"></a><a id="17599" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17599" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-sp</a> <a id="17617" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17619" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17620" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17620" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17622" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17624" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="17632" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17634" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17634" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="17636" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17638" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17620" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17640" href="universes.html#758" class="Function Operator">̇</a><a id="17641" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17643" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17643" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="17645" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17647" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1088" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="17652" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17653" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#781" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="17661" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17620" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17663" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="17664" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="17666" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2005" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="17669" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17620" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17670" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="17673" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17675" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a> <a id="17683" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17684" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2005" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="17687" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17620" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17688" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17690" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17691" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2005" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="17694" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17620" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17695" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="17698" class="Symbol">→</a>                  <a id="17717" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#3890" class="Function">class-product</a><a id="17730" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17731" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17620" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17732" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17734" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17620" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17735" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17737" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17634" class="Bound">X</a><a id="17738" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17740" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17741" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3089" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="17743" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17643" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="17744" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17746" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2725" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="17748" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3089" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="17749" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17750" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3830" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="17752" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17643" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="17753" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="17755" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17599" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-sp</a> <a id="17773" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17773" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="17777" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17779" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14292" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a><a id="17784" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17785" class="Argument">hfe</a> <a id="17789" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17791" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17773" class="Bound">hfe</a><a id="17794" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17796" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16880" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a>
